CREATE TABLE `address` (
  `Code` int(255) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `CodeLocality` int(255) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `CodeStreet` int(255) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `StreetName` varchar(255) COLLATE utf32_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `House` varchar(20) COLLATE utf32_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `Building` varchar(10) COLLATE utf32_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `Apartment` varchar(20) COLLATE utf32_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Code`),
  KEY `Street_FK` (`CodeStreet`),
  KEY `Locality_FK` (`CodeLocality`),
  CONSTRAINT `Locality_FK` FOREIGN KEY (`CodeLocality`) REFERENCES `locality` (`Code`) ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `Street_FK` FOREIGN KEY (`CodeStreet`) REFERENCES `street` (`Code`) ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf32 COLLATE=utf32_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE `order` (
  `Code` int(255) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `Notes` varchar(255) COLLATE utf32_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `CodeState` int(255) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `CodeAdress` int(255) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,

  CONSTRAINT `Customer_FK` FOREIGN KEY (`CodeCustomer`) REFERENCES `customer` (`Code`) ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `State_FK` FOREIGN KEY (`CodeState`) REFERENCES `state` (`Code`) ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf32 COLLATE=utf32_unicode_ci;
